    69                          !macro note .pitch, .dur {
    70                              !if (.dur = 1) {
    71                                  .durIndex = 0
    72                              }
    73                              !if (.dur = 2) {
    74                                  .durIndex = 1
    75                              }
    76                              !if (.dur = 3) {
    77                                  .durIndex = 2
    78                              }
    79                              !if (.dur = 4) {
    80                                  .durIndex = 3
    81                              }
    82                              !if (.dur = 6) {
    83                                  .durIndex = 4
    84                              }
    85                              !if (.dur = 7) {
    86                                  .durIndex = 5
    87                              }
    88                              !if (.dur = 9) {
    89                                  .durIndex = 6
    90                              }
    91                              !if (.dur = 12) {
    92                                  .durIndex = 7
    93                              }
    94                              !ifndef .durIndex {
    95                                  !error "Unknown duration"
    96                              }
    97                              !byte .pitch + 32 * .durIndex
    98                          }

   100                          !macro end_melody {
   101                              !byte 0
   102                          }
   103                          
   104                          ; ***************************************************************************************
   105                          ; os variables
   106                          irq_accumulator                                     = $fc
   107                          irq1_vector_low                                     = $0204
   108                          irq1_vector_high                                    = $0205
   109                          
   110                          crtcAddressRegister                                 = $fe00     ;
   111                          crtcAddressWrite                                    = $fe01     ;
   112                          
   113                          ; ***************************************************************************************
   114                          ; Video ULA Register
   115                          ;         bits 765: determines cursor width
   116                          ;         bit    4: 0 = 40 bytes per scan line, 1 = 80 bytes per scan line
   117                          ;         bits  32: number of columns (%00=10 columns, %01=20, %10=40, %11=80)
   118                          ;            bit 1: teletext (1=enabled, 0=disabled)
   119                          ;            bit 0: current flashing colour state
   120                          videoULARegister                                    = $fe20
   121                          videoULAPaletteRegister                             = $fe21     ; Video ULA palette register
   122                          
   123                          ; ***************************************************************************************
   124                          ; Write to System VIA, register B
   125                          ; On Entry:
   126                          ;     Interrupts must already be disabled
   127                          ;     A = value to write (0-15)
   128                          ;
   129                          ; Notes:
   130                          ;     Values 0-15 can be written to System VIA Port B:
   131                          ;
   132                          ;         Value   Effect
   133                          ;         -------------------------
   134                          ;         0       Enable sound chip
   135                          ;         1       Disable Read Speech
   136                          ;         2       Disable Write Speech
   137                          ;         3       Disable Keyboard write
   138                          ;         4       Hardware scrolling - set C0=0 (See below)
   139                          ;         5       Hardware scrolling - set C1=0 (See below)
   140                          ;         6       Turn on Caps LED
   141                          ;         7       Turn on Shift LED
   142                          ;         8       Disable sound chip
   143                          ;         9       Enable Read Speech
   144                          ;         10      Enable Write Speech
   145                          ;         11      Enable Keyboard write
   146                          ;         12      Hardware scrolling - set C0=1 (See below)
   147                          ;         13      Hardware scrolling - set C1=1 (See below)
   148                          ;         14      Turn off Caps LED
   149                          ;         15      Turn off Shift LED
   150                          ;
   151                          ; If C0=0 and C1=1 then hardware scrolling starts at $5800
   152                          ;
   153                          systemVIADataDirectionRegisterA                     = $fe43     ; System VIA data direction register A (DDRA)
   154                          systemVIARegisterANoHandshake                       = $fe4f     ; System VIA Register A without handshaking
   155                          
   156                          systemVIARegisterB                                  = $fe40     ;
   157                          systemVIATimer1CounterLow                           = $fe44     ;
   158                          systemVIATimer1CounterHigh                          = $fe45     ;
   159                          systemVIATimer1LatchLow                             = $fe46     ;
   160                          systemVIATimer1LatchHigh                            = $fe47     ;
   161                          systemVIAAuxiliaryControlRegister                   = $fe4b     ;
   162                          systemVIAInterruptFlagRegister                      = $fe4d     ;
   163                          systemVIAInterruptEnableRegister                    = $fe4e     ;
   164                          
   165                          
   166                          userVIATimer1CounterLow                             = $fe64     ; Timer 1 counter (low)
   167                          userVIATimer1CounterHigh                            = $fe65     ; Timer 1 counter (high)
   168                          userVIATimer1LatchLow                               = $fe66     ; Timer 1 latch (low)
   169                          userVIATimer1LatchHigh                              = $fe67     ; Timer 1 latch (high)
   170                          userVIAAuxiliaryControlRegister                     = $fe6b     ; auxiliary control register
   171                          userVIAInterruptFlagRegister                        = $fe6d     ; Interrupt flag register
   172                          userVIAInterruptEnableRegister                      = $fe6e     ; Interrupt enable register
   173                          
   174                          OSBYTE                                              = $fff4     ; used during program initialization only
   175                          
   176                          ; physical colours
   177                          black   = 0
   178                          red     = 1
   179                          green   = 2
   180                          yellow  = 3
   181                          blue    = 4
   182                          magenta = 5
   183                          cyan    = 6
   184                          white   = 7
   185                          
   186                          ; ***************************************************************************************
   187                          ; This is the number of timer ticks per frame (num PAL scanlines * 64us/line)
   188                          ; This timing is only true of non-interlaced modes.
   189                          ; We have to subtract 2 because the latch reload costs 2us.
   190                          ; This is not documented anywhere!
   191                          FramePeriod     = 312*64-2
   192                          
   193                          ; Calculate here the timer value to interrupt at the desired line
   194                          Timer1Value      = 76*64 + 39
   195                          
   196                          ; This is the delay between interrupts (one character row = 8 pixel rows)
   197                          ShortTimerValue  = 8*64 - 2
   198

   503                          ; ***************************************************************************************
   504                          initialise_room
   505  0208 201f02                 jsr initialise_room_data                        ;
   506  020b 20a104                 jsr initialise_enemies                          ;
   507  020e 20334d                 jsr initialise_arrows                           ;
   508  0211 20c512                 jsr calculate_screen_address_of_conveyor        ;
   509  0214 201554                 jsr plot_enemies                                ; [not really needed, but may be useful for screenshots]
   510  0217 a940                   lda #64                                         ; default to half stride
   511  0219 8de14c                 sta life_sprite_address_low                     ;
   512  021c 4ce04c                 jmp force_update_lives                          ;
   513                          
   514                          ; ***************************************************************************************
   515                          initialise_room_data
   516  021f a900                   lda #0                                          ;
   517  0221 8552                   sta room_data_offset                            ;
   518  0223 8553                   sta bits_remaining_in_room_data_byte            ;
   519  0225 859f                   sta player_rope_pixel                           ;
   520  0227 8557                   sta game_timer                                  ;
   521  0229 a655                   ldx player_room                                 ;
   522  022b 207212                 jsr calculate_room_data_address                 ;
   523  022e a028                   ldy #>($7e00-screen_memory_start)               ;
   524  0230 20ee16                 jsr clear_screen_y                              ;
   525  0233 201605                 jsr initialise_room_items_and_exits             ;
   526  0236 205105                 jsr initialise_room_background_tiles_and_title  ;
   527  0239 a9ee                   lda #$ee                                        ;
   528  023b 855f                   sta rope_position                               ;
   529  023d a9ff                   lda #$ff                                        ;
   530  023f 8567                   sta item_number                                 ;
   531  0241 855c                   sta rope_velocity_relative_to_centre            ;
   532  0243 855b                   sta rope_position_relative_to_centre            ;
   533  0245 a901                   lda #1                                          ;
   534  0247 859c                   sta player_not_plotted                          ; Mark player as not needing to be unplotted
   535  0249 a59d                   lda out_of_time                                 ;
   536  024b 8563                   sta player_killed                               ;

   853                          ; ***************************************************************************************
   854                          ;
   855                          ; On Entry:
   856                          ;   X is the base direction
   857                          ;
   858                          ; Directions are:
   859                          ;   0 = right
   860                          ;   1 = up
   861                          ;   2 = left
   862                          ;   3 = down
   863                          ;   8 = right and up diagonal
   864                          ;   9 = left and up diagonal
   865                          ;  10 = right and down diagonal
   866                          ;  11 = left and down diagonal
   867                          ;

   931                          initialise_enemies

   937                          initialise_enemies_loop                             ; For each enemy,
   938  04ab a206                   ldx #6                                          ; Get six bits of room data for sprite
   939  04ad 20b602                 jsr get_x_bits_of_room_data                     ;
   940  04b0 994455                 sta enemies_sprite,Y                            ;
   941  04b3 a205                   ldx #5                                          ; Get five bits of room data for x position
   942  04b5 20d802                 jsr get_x_bits_of_room_data_multiplied_by_eight ;
   943  04b8 995f55                 sta enemies_x,Y                                 ;
   944  04bb a204                   ldx #4                                          ; Get four bits of room data for y position
   945  04bd 20d802                 jsr get_x_bits_of_room_data_multiplied_by_eight ;
   946  04c0 996855                 sta enemies_y,Y                                 ;
   947  04c3 a205                   ldx #5                                          ; Get five bits of room data for minimum position

   949  04c8 997a55                 sta enemies_minimum,Y                           ;
   950  04cb a205                   ldx #5                                          ; Get five bits of room data for maximum position
   951  04cd 20d802                 jsr get_x_bits_of_room_data_multiplied_by_eight ;
   952  04d0 998355                 sta enemies_maximum,Y                           ;
   953  04d3 20ac02                 jsr get_one_bit_of_room_data                    ; direction (0 = horizontal, 1 = vertical)
   954  04d6 0a                     asl                                             ;
   955  04d7 f00b                   beq horizontal                                  ;
   956  04d9 b98355                 lda enemies_maximum,Y                           ; }
   957  04dc 18                     clc                                             ; }
   958  04dd 6901                   adc #1                                          ; } vertical monsters maximum is one more than the multiple of eight
   959  04df 998355                 sta enemies_maximum,Y                           ; }
   960  04e2 a9ff                   lda #$ff                                        ;
   961                          horizontal
   962  04e4 995655                 sta enemies_direction,Y                         ;
   963  04e7 20ac02                 jsr get_one_bit_of_room_data                    ; direction (0 = left/up, 1=right/down)
   964  04ea 8597                   sta invert                                      ;

   966  04ee 20b602                 jsr get_x_bits_of_room_data                     ;

   973  04fd 997155                 sta enemies_speed,Y                             ;
   974                          skip_inversion5

  1255

  1267  06e0 88                     dey                                             ;

  1269

  1271  06e3 a5a5                   lda temp_address_low                            ; }

  1277                          +

  1291                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  1292                          ;
  1293                          ; On entry: A = bit pattern: abcdefgh
  1294                          ; On exit:  A = bit pattern: dcbahgfe
  1295                          ;
  1296                          ; 19 instructions, 28 bytes, 46 cycles (assuming temp_reverse is in zero page, and including RTS).
  1297                          ;
  1298                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  1299                          reverse_each_nybble
  1300  06fe aa                     tax                                             ; X = abcdefgh
  1301  06ff 29aa                   and #$aa                                        ; A = a0c0e0g0
  1302  0701 4a                     lsr                                             ; A = 0a0c0e0g
  1303  0702 85ac                   sta temp_reverse                                ; t = 0a0c0e0g
  1304  0704 8a                     txa                                             ; A = abcdefgh
  1305  0705 0a                     asl                                             ; A = bcdefgh0
  1306  0706 29aa                   and #$aa                                        ; A = b0d0f0h0
  1307  0708 05ac                   ora temp_reverse                                ; A = badcfehg
  1308  070a aa                     tax                                             ; X = badcfehg
  1309  070b 2933                   and #$33                                        ; A = 00dc00hg
  1310  070d 0a                     asl                                             ; A = 0dc00hg0
  1311  070e 0a                     asl                                             ; A = dc00hg00
  1312  070f 85ac                   sta temp_reverse                                ; t = dc00hg00
  1313  0711 8a                     txa                                             ; A = badcfehg
  1314  0712 4a                     lsr                                             ; A = 0badcfeh
  1315  0713 4a                     lsr                                             ; A = 00badcfe
  1316  0714 2933                   and #$33                                        ; A = 00ba00fe
  1317  0716 05ac                   ora temp_reverse                                ; A = dcbahgfe
  1318  0718 60                     rts                                             ;
  1319                          
  1320                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  1321                          unpack_enemy_sprite
  1322  0719 a000                   ldy #0                                          ; loop counter for target (increments)
  1323  071b a21f                   ldx #31                                         ; loop counter for source (decrementing)
  1324                          unpack_enemy_sprite_loop
  1325  071d 8c2d07                 sty tempY                                       ; remember Y
  1326  0720 8a                     txa                                             ;
  1327  0721 a8                     tay                                             ; Y = X
  1328  0722 b1c8                   lda (sprite_address_low1),Y                     ; get byte from 1bpp sprite
  1329  0724 205007                 jsr unpack_byte_of_sprite_data                  ; unpack into two bytes of 2bpp data
  1330  0727 a488                   ldy unpacked_byte_two                           ; }
  1331  0729 8588                   sta unpacked_byte_two                           ; } swap A and unpacked_byte_two
  1332  072b 98                     tya                                             ; }
  1333                          tempY = * + 1
  1334  072c a0ff                   ldy #$ff                                        ; recall Y
  1335  072e 9184                   sta (unpacked_sprite_address_low),Y             ; store first of two bytes
  1336  0730 c8                     iny                                             ;
  1337  0731 a588                   lda unpacked_byte_two                           ;

  1339  0735 c8                     iny                                             ;
  1340  0736 ca                     dex                                             ;
  1341  0737 10e4                   bpl unpack_enemy_sprite_loop                    ;
  1342                          
  1343  0739 a5c8                   lda sprite_address_low1                         ;
  1344  073b 18                     clc                                             ;
  1345  073c 6920                   adc #32                                         ;
  1346  073e 85c8                   sta sprite_address_low1                         ; add 32 to source address
  1347  0740 9002                   bcc +                                           ;
  1348  0742 e6c9                   inc sprite_address_high1                        ;
  1349                          +
  1350  0744 a584                   lda unpacked_sprite_address_low                 ;
  1351  0746 18                     clc                                             ;
  1352  0747 6940                   adc #64                                         ;
  1353  0749 8584                   sta unpacked_sprite_address_low                 ; add 64 to destination address
  1354  074b 9002                   bcc +                                           ;
  1355  074d e685                   inc unpacked_sprite_address_high                ;
  1356                          +
  1357  074f 60                     rts                                             ;
  1358                          
  1359                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  1360                          unpack_byte_of_sprite_data
  1361  0750 8592                   sta packed_byte1                                ;
  1362  0752 29f0                   and #$f0                                        ;
  1363  0754 854c                   sta tmp2                                        ;
  1364  0756 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  1365  0757 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  1366  0758 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  1367  0759 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  1368  075a 054c                   ora tmp2                                        ;
  1369  075c 8588                   sta unpacked_byte_two                           ;
  1370  075e a592                   lda packed_byte1                                ;
  1371  0760 290f                   and #$0f                                        ;
  1372  0762 854c                   sta tmp2                                        ;
  1373  0764 0a                     asl                                             ;
  1374  0765 0a                     asl                                             ;
  1375  0766 0a                     asl                                             ;
  1376  0767 0a                     asl                                             ;

  1380                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  1381                          ;
  1382                          ; On Entry:
  1383                          ;  A holds the X coordinate in pixels
  1384                          ;  X holds the Y coordinate in pixels
  1385                          ;
  1386                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  1387                          calculate_screen_address
  1388  076b 29fc                   and #$fc                                        ; lose the lower two bits
  1389  076d 0a                     asl                                             ; shift up
  1390  076e 85fe                   sta screen_address_low                          ; store
  1391  0770 26ff                   rol screen_address_high                         ; carry into high byte
  1392                          
  1393  0772 8a                     txa                                             ;

  1398                          
  1399  077a 8a                     txa                                             ;
  1400  077b 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  1401  077c 4a                     lsr                                             ;

  3515                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  3516                          ;
  3517                          ; Send byte to sound chip
  3518                          ;
  3519                          ; On Entry:
  3520                          ;   A = byte to send
  3521                          ;
  3522                          ; On Exit:
  3523                          ;   Preserves X
  3524                          ;
  3525                          ; Notes:
  3526                          ; To write pitch P (10 bit integer) to channel C (0-2, or 3=noise) and set volume V:
  3527                          ;
  3528                          ; write first byte:   128 + 32*C + top four bits of pitch P (0-15)
  3529                          ; write second byte:  lower 6 bits of pitch P
  3530                          ;
  3531                          ; To set volume V (0-15) on channel C (0-2, or 3=noise):
  3532                          ; write volume byte:  128 + 32*C + 16 + volume (0-15, 0 = loudest)
  3533                          ;
  3534                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  3535                          send_to_sound_chip
  3536  1433 842d                   sty sound_temp_y                                    ;
  3537  1435 a0ff                   ldy #$ff                                            ; }
  3538  1437 8c43fe                 sty systemVIADataDirectionRegisterA                 ; } set data direction to all outputs
  3539  143a 8d4ffe                 sta systemVIARegisterANoHandshake                   ; send data byte to sound chip
  3540  143d c8                     iny                                                 ; Y=0
  3541  143e 8c40fe                 sty systemVIARegisterB                              ; set the write enable line low (active)
  3542                                                                                  ; to let the sound chip know there
  3543                                                                                  ; is data
  3544  1441 204b14                 jsr +                                               ; execute a short delay (this is to
  3545                                                                                  ; keep the write enable line low for
  3546                                                                                  ; at least 8 us, 16 cycles. This is
  3547                                                                                  ; required by the sound chip hardware)
  3548  1444 a008                   ldy #8                                              ; }
  3549  1446 8c40fe                 sty systemVIARegisterB                              ; } pull the write enable line high (inactive)
  3550  1449 a42d                   ldy sound_temp_y                                    ;
  3551                          +
  3552  144b 60                     rts                                                 ;
  3553                          
  3554                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  3555                          ; tile_table is a 32x16 byte array, one byte for each tile in the playfield:
  3556                          ;
  3557                          ;     $80       Empty space
  3558                          ;     $81 + N   Enemy N     (0 <= N < 8)
  3559                          ;     $01       Platform
  3560                          ;     $02       Wall
  3561                          ;     $03       Slope
  3562                          ;     $04       Conveyor
  3563                          ;     $C5       Deadly
  3564                          ;     $D0 + N   Item N      (0 <= N < 12)
  3565                          ;
  3566                          ; This can be interpreted as the top four bits are the broad tile type,
  3567                          ; and the bottom 4 bits are the index within that type
  3568                          ;
  3569                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  3570                          tile_table

  3646                          clear_screen
  3647  16ec a02a                   ldy #>($8000-screen_memory_start)               ;
  3648                          clear_screen_y
  3649  16ee a956                   lda #>screen_memory_start                       ;
  3650  16f0 8df816                 sta clear_screen_loop + 2                       ;
  3651  16f3 a200                   ldx #0                                          ;
  3652  16f5 8a                     txa                                             ;
  3653                          clear_screen_loop
  3654  16f6 9d0056                 sta screen_memory_start,x                       ;
  3655  16f9 e8                     inx                                             ;
  3656  16fa d0fa                   bne clear_screen_loop                           ;
  3657  16fc eef816                 inc clear_screen_loop + 2                       ;
  3658  16ff 88                     dey                                             ;

  3937                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  3938                          ; This commented out data is what the jump parabola should be, but the engine has trouble

  4913  4e87 f525                   sbc sound_duration_for_channel_x,X          ;

  5440                          update_music
  5441  5290 c6d8                   dec music_timer                                 ;
  5442  5292 a599                   lda melody_active                               ;
  5443  5294 f013                   beq leave29                                     ;
  5444  5296 a5d9                   lda pre_tune_delay                              ;
  5445  5298 f003                   beq +                                           ;
  5446  529a c6d9                   dec pre_tune_delay                              ;
  5447  529c 60                     rts                                             ;
  5448                          +
  5449  529d a4d6                   ldy tune_number                                 ;
  5450  529f b97252                 lda channels_in_each_tune,Y                     ;
  5451  52a2 a8                     tay                                             ;
  5452                          -
  5453  52a3 20aa52                 jsr update_music_channel_y                      ;
  5454  52a6 88                     dey                                             ;
  5455  52a7 10fa                   bpl -                                           ;
  5456                          leave29
  5457  52a9 60                     rts                                             ;
  5458                          
  5459                          update_music_channel_y
  5460  52aa a517                   lda music_enabled                               ;
  5461  52ac f0fb                   beq leave29                                     ;
  5462  52ae b6cd                   ldx note_length,Y                               ;
  5463  52b0 ca                     dex
  5464  52b1 96cd                   stx note_length,Y                               ;
  5465  52b3 d069                   bne set_melody_vol                              ;
  5466                          
  5467  52b5 98                     tya                                             ;
  5468  52b6 18                     clc                                             ;
  5469  52b7 65d6                   adc tune_number                                 ;
  5470  52b9 aa                     tax                                             ;
  5471  52ba bd7f52                 lda tune_addresses_low,X                        ;
  5472  52bd 8dcf52                 sta tune_address1_low                           ;
  5473  52c0 8d0e53                 sta tune_address2_low                           ;
  5474  52c3 bd8352                 lda tune_addresses_high,X                       ;
  5475  52c6 8dd052                 sta tune_address1_high                          ;
  5476  52c9 8d0f53                 sta tune_address2_high                          ;
  5477                          
  5478  52cc b6ca                   ldx note_number,Y                               ;
  5479                          tune_address1_low  = * + 1
  5480                          tune_address1_high = * + 2
  5481  52ce bd0001                 lda rich_man_table,X                            ;
  5482  52d1 8511                   sta music_note_byte                             ; push music byte
  5483  52d3 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5484  52d4 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5485  52d5 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5486  52d6 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5487  52d7 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5488  52d8 aa                     tax                                             ;
  5489  52d9 bd7752                 lda duration_table,X                            ;
  5490  52dc b6ca                   ldx note_number,Y                               ;
  5491  52de 24d7                   bit tune_speed                                  ;
  5492  52e0 3001                   bmi +                                           ;
  5493  52e2 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5494                          +
  5495  52e3 99cd00                 sta note_length,Y                               ;
  5496  52e6 a511                   lda music_note_byte                             ; music byte
  5497  52e8 291f                   and #$1f                                        ;
  5498  52ea c91f                   cmp #non                                        ;
  5499  52ec f05a                   beq start_rapid_decay                           ;
  5500  52ee a201                   ldx #1                                          ;
  5501  52f0 96d3                   stx note_decay_amount,Y                         ;
  5502  52f2 aa                     tax                                             ;
  5503  52f3 bd9801                 lda pitch_table_first,X                         ;
  5504  52f6 18                     clc                                             ;
  5505  52f7 797452                 adc channel_pitch_adjust,Y                      ;
  5506  52fa 203314                 jsr send_to_sound_chip                          ; first byte
  5507  52fd bdb701                 lda pitch_table_second,X                        ;
  5508  5300 203314                 jsr send_to_sound_chip                          ; second byte
  5509                          
  5510  5303 a92c                   lda #11 * 4                                     ; initial volume
  5511  5305 99d000                 sta note_volume,Y                               ;
  5512                          
  5513                          next_note
  5514  5308 b6ca                   ldx note_number,Y                               ;
  5515  530a e8                     inx                                             ;
  5516  530b 96ca                   stx note_number,Y                               ;
  5517                          tune_address2_low  = * + 1
  5518                          tune_address2_high = * + 2
  5519  530d bd0001                 lda rich_man_table,X                            ;
  5520  5310 c900                   cmp #0                                          ;
  5521  5312 d00a                   bne set_melody_vol                              ;
  5522                          
  5523                              ; restart tune
  5524  5314 a900                   lda #0                                          ;
  5525  5316 99ca00                 sta note_number,Y                               ;
  5526  5319 a901                   lda #1                                          ;
  5527  531b 99cd00                 sta note_length,Y                               ;
  5528                          set_melody_vol
  5529                              ; set volume of playing note
  5530                              ; To set volume V (0-15) on channel C (0-2, or 3=noise):
  5531                              ; write volume byte:  128 + 32*C + 16 + volume (0-15, 0 = loudest)
  5532                          
  5533  531e b9d000                 lda note_volume,Y                               ;
  5534  5321 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5535  5322 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5536  5323 596953                 eor volume_for_channel,Y                        ;
  5537  5326 203314                 jsr send_to_sound_chip                          ; volume byte
  5538                          
  5539                              ; update volume
  5540  5329 c000                   cpy #0                                          ;
  5541  532b f006                   beq +                                           ; if (channel 0) then branch (decay at normal rate)
  5542  532d a5d8                   lda music_timer                                 ; }
  5543  532f 2903                   and #3                                          ; } decay slowly
  5544  5331 d014                   bne leave31                                     ; }
  5545                          +
  5546  5333 b9d000                 lda note_volume,Y                               ;
  5547  5336 38                     sec
  5548  5337 f9d300                 sbc note_decay_amount,Y                         ;
  5549  533a 99d000                 sta note_volume,Y                               ;
  5550                          
  5551  533d b9d000                 lda note_volume,Y                               ;
  5552  5340 1005                   bpl leave31                                     ;
  5553                          
  5554  5342 a900                   lda #0                                          ;
  5555  5344 99d000                 sta note_volume,Y                               ;
  5556                          leave31
  5557  5347 60                     rts                                             ;
  5558                          
  5559                          start_rapid_decay
  5560  5348 a904                   lda #4                                          ;
  5561  534a 99d300                 sta note_decay_amount,Y                         ;
  5562  534d d0b9                   bne next_note                                   ;
  5563                          
  5564                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  5565                          check_for_q_and_s_keys

  5567  5351 f004                   beq s_not_pressed                               ;
  5568  5353 a901                   lda #1                                          ;
  5569  5355 8517                   sta music_enabled                               ;
  5570                          s_not_pressed

  5572  5359 f00d                   beq q_not_pressed                               ;
  5573  535b a900                   lda #0                                          ;
  5574  535d 8517                   sta music_enabled                               ;
  5575  535f 4c8752                 jmp silence_tune                                ;

  5579                          q_not_pressed

  5589                          ; Change the appearance of logical colour Y to physical colour A
  5590                          set_logical_colour_y_to_a
  5591  536c 4907                   eor #7                                          ;
  5592  536e 197648                 ora paletteLookupTable,Y                        ;
  5593  5371 8d21fe                 sta videoULAPaletteRegister                     ; store actual colour in register
  5594  5374 4910                   eor #$10                                        ;
  5595  5376 8d21fe                 sta videoULAPaletteRegister                     ; store actual colour in register
  5596  5379 4950                   eor #$50                                        ;
  5597  537b 8d21fe                 sta videoULAPaletteRegister                     ; store actual colour in register
  5598  537e 4910                   eor #$10                                        ;
  5599  5380 8d21fe                 sta videoULAPaletteRegister                     ; store actual colour in register
  5600  5383 60                     rts                                             ;
  5601                          
  5602                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  5603                          irq_routine
  5604  5384 8a                     txa                                             ;
  5605  5385 48                     pha                                             ;
  5606  5386 98                     tya                                             ;
  5607  5387 48                     pha                                             ;
  5608                          
  5609  5388 ad4dfe                 lda systemVIAInterruptFlagRegister              ; get interrupt flag register
  5610  538b 29c0                   and #$c0                                        ;
  5611  538d c9c0                   cmp #$c0                                        ;
  5612  538f d053                   bne exit_irq                                    ; unknown interrupt
  5613  5391 8d4dfe                 sta systemVIAInterruptFlagRegister              ; clear interrupt
  5614                          
  5615  5394 a600                   ldx irq_counter                                 ;
  5616  5396 e8                     inx                                             ;
  5617  5397 e027                   cpx #39                                         ;
  5618  5399 9008                   bcc +                                           ;
  5619  539b 20a54e                 jsr update_sound                                ; update all audio
  5620  539e 209052                 jsr update_music                                ;
  5621  53a1 a200                   ldx #0                                          ;
  5622                          +
  5623  53a3 8600                   stx irq_counter                                 ;
  5624  53a5 e010                   cpx #16                                         ;
  5625  53a7 d007                   bne +                                           ;
  5626  53a9 e601                   inc vsync_counter                               ;
  5627  53ab a904                   lda #4                                          ; change to footer palette
  5628  53ad 4cd153                 jmp change_all_palette                          ;
  5629                          
  5630                          +
  5631  53b0 b00e                   bcs +                                           ;
  5632                              ; apply palette changes in rows 0-15
  5633  53b2 b5da                   lda palette_changes,X                           ;
  5634  53b4 302e                   bmi exit_irq                                    ;
  5635  53b6 2903                   and #3                                          ;
  5636  53b8 a8                     tay                                             ;
  5637  53b9 b5da                   lda palette_changes,X                           ;
  5638  53bb 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5639  53bc 4a                     lsr                                             ;
  5640  53bd 206c53                 jsr set_logical_colour_y_to_a                   ;
  5641                          
  5642                          +
  5643  53c0 e014                   cpx #20                                         ;
  5644  53c2 d007                   bne +                                           ;
  5645                          
  5646                              ; final row
  5647  53c4 a003                   ldy #3                                          ;
  5648  53c6 a907                   lda #white                                      ;
  5649  53c8 206c53                 jsr set_logical_colour_y_to_a                   ;
  5650                          
  5651                          +
  5652  53cb e015                   cpx #21                                         ;
  5653  53cd d015                   bne exit_irq                                    ;
  5654                          
  5655                          change_all_room_palette
  5656  53cf a900                   lda #0                                          ; change to room palette
  5657                          +
  5658                          change_all_palette
  5659  53d1 18                     clc                                             ;
  5660  53d2 6966                   adc #<room_palette                              ;
  5661  53d4 8dda53                 sta change_palette_low                          ;
  5662  53d7 a000                   ldy #0                                          ;
  5663                          -
  5664                          change_palette_low = * + 1
  5665  53d9 b96648                 lda room_palette,Y                              ;
  5666  53dc 206c53                 jsr set_logical_colour_y_to_a                   ;
  5667  53df c8                     iny                                             ;
  5668  53e0 c004                   cpy #4                                          ;
  5669  53e2 d0f5                   bne -                                           ;
  5670                          
  5671                          exit_irq
  5672  53e4 68                     pla                                             ;
  5673  53e5 a8                     tay                                             ;
  5674  53e6 68                     pla                                             ;
  5675  53e7 aa                     tax                                             ;
  5676  53e8 a5fc                   lda irq_accumulator                             ;
  5677  53ea 40                     rti                                             ;
  5678                          
  5679                          !if ((>room_palette) != (>(room_palette + 4))) {
  5680                              !error "Alignment of room_palette is wrong"
  5681                          }

  5762                          
  5763                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  5764                          ; Each pixel of the rope is at an offset from the previous one.
  5765                          ; X and Y offsets are given in the following two tables.
  5766                          ; The rope is animated by starting to draw the rope at different offsets into these tables
  5767                          ; (a sliding window). The first set of entries in each table are all the same so we deal
  5768                          ; with that in code. The full uncompressed table is 86 entries:
  5769                          ;
  5770                          ; rope_position    dx    dy
  5771                          ; -------------------------
  5772                          ; $d4               0     3
  5773                          ; $d5               0     3
  5774                          ; $d6               0     3
  5775                          ; $d7               0     3
  5776                          ; $d8               0     3
  5777                          ; $d9               0     3
  5778                          ; $da               0     3
  5779                          ; $db               0     3
  5780                          ; $dc               0     3
  5781                          ; $dd               0     3
  5782                          ; $de               0     3
  5783                          ; $df               0     3
  5784                          ; $e0               0     3
  5785                          ; $e1               0     3
  5786                          ; $e2               0     3
  5787                          ; $e3               0     3
  5788                          ; $e4               0     3
  5789                          ; $e5               0     3
  5790                          ; $e6               0     3
  5791                          ; $e7               0     3
  5792                          ; $e8               0     3
  5793                          ; $e9               0     3
  5794                          ; $ea               0     3
  5795                          ; $eb               0     3
  5796                          ; $ec               0     3
  5797                          ; $ed               0     3
  5798                          ; $ee               0     3
  5799                          ; $ef               0     3
  5800                          ; $f0               0     3
  5801                          ; $f1               0     3
  5802                          ; $f2               0     3
  5803                          ; $f3               0     3
  5804                          ; $f4               1     3
  5805                          ; $f5               1     3
  5806                          ; $f6               1     3
  5807                          ; $f7               1     3
  5808                          ; $f8               1     3
  5809                          ; $f9               1     3
  5810                          ; $fa               1     3
  5811                          ; $fb               1     3
  5812                          ; $fc               1     3
  5813                          ; $fd               1     3
  5814                          ; $fe               1     3
  5815                          ; $ff               1     3
  5816                          ; $00               2     3
  5817                          ; $01               2     3
  5818                          ; $02               2     3
  5819                          ; $03               2     3

  5862  5444 0202010202010102...    !byte 2,2,1,2, 2,1,1,2, 1,1,2,2, 3,2,3,2, 3,3,3,3

  6075                          !if (* > screen_memory_start) {
  6076                              !error "Code too long by ", * - screen_memory_start
  6077                          }
  6078                          free_before_screen = screen_memory_start - end_of_real_code
  6079                          
  6080                          !pseudopc * - $0208 + $1100 {
  6081                          
  6082                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  6083                          ;
  6084                          ; everything from here on is initialisation code run only once, then becomes part of the
  6085                          ; screen memory.
  6086                          ;
  6087                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  6088                          
  6089                          
  6090                          ; ***************************************************************************************
  6091                          entry_point
  6092  55f3 a98c                   lda #140                                        ;
  6093  55f5 a20c                   ldx #12                                         ; *TAPE
  6094  55f7 20f4ff                 jsr OSBYTE                                      ;
  6095                          
  6096  55fa a9c8                   lda #$c8                                        ; Write BREAK/ESCAPE effect
  6097  55fc a203                   ldx #3                                          ; Normal ESCAPE effect, Memory cleared on next reset
  6098  55fe 20f4ff                 jsr OSBYTE                                      ;
  6099                          
  6100  5601 a900                   lda #0                                          ;
  6101  5603 854b                   sta replay_timer                                ;
  6102                          
  6103  5605 78                     sei                                             ;
  6104  5606 a2ff                   ldx #$ff                                        ; } reset the stack pointer
  6105  5608 9a                     txs                                             ; }
  6106                          
  6107  5609 a9aa                   lda #$aa                                        ; }
  6108  560b a200                   ldx #0                                          ; }
  6109                          -                                                   ; }
  6110  560d ca                     dex                                             ; } just for debugging purposes, fill page 1
  6111  560e 9d0001                 sta $0100,X                                     ; } (below the stack) with $aa
  6112  5611 d0fa                   bne -                                           ; }
  6113                          
  6114  5613 a2d6                   ldx #copy_melody_end - copy_melody              ; }
  6115                          -                                                   ; }
  6116  5615 ca                     dex                                             ; }
  6117  5616 bd1d66                 lda copy_melody,X                               ; }
  6118  5619 9d0001                 sta $0100,X                                     ; }
  6119  561c e000                   cpx #0                                          ; }
  6120  561e d0f5                   bne -                                           ; }
  6121                          
  6122                              ; relocate code
  6123  5620 78                     sei                                             ;
  6124  5621 a000                   ldy #<$1100                                     ;
  6125  5623 8470                   sty $70                                         ;
  6126  5625 a211                   ldx #>$1100                                     ;
  6127  5627 8671                   stx $71                                         ; Copy code from $1100 to $0208
  6128                          
  6129  5629 a008                   ldy #<$0208                                     ;
  6130  562b 8472                   sty $72                                         ;
  6131  562d a202                   ldx #>$0208                                     ;
  6132  562f 8673                   stx $73                                         ;
  6133                          
  6134  5631 a254                   ldx #>(end_of_real_code - $0208 + $ff)          ; loop counter (copy as many pages as we need)
  6135  5633 a000                   ldy #0                                          ;
  6136                          -
  6137  5635 b170                   lda ($70),y                                     ;
  6138  5637 9172                   sta ($72),y                                     ; copy a page of memory
  6139  5639 c8                     iny                                             ;
  6140  563a d0f9                   bne -                                           ;
  6141                          
  6142  563c e671                   inc $71                                         ;
  6143  563e e673                   inc $73                                         ; increment high byte of source and destination
  6144                          
  6145  5640 ca                     dex                                             ; decrement loop counter
  6146  5641 d0f2                   bne -                                           ; if (not done yet) then branch back
  6147                          
  6148                              ; set custom mode 1
  6149                              ; Set hardware scrolling value
  6150  5643 a904                   lda #4                                          ; Set C0=0
  6151  5645 8d40fe                 sta systemVIARegisterB                          ; Setting the address for hardware scrolling
  6152  5648 a90d                   lda #13                                         ; Set C1=1
  6153  564a 8d40fe                 sta systemVIARegisterB                          ; Set Hardware scrolling address (C0=1,C1=1 i.e. $3000)
  6154                          
  6155                              ; Set Video ULA register
  6156  564d a9d8                   lda #%11011000                                  ;
  6157  564f 8d20fe                 sta videoULARegister                            ; write to control register
  6158                          
  6159                              ; set video ULA
  6160  5652 a9d8                   lda #%11011000                                  ;
  6161  5654 8d20fe                 sta videoULARegister                            ;
  6162                          
  6163                              ; Write to all 16 registers of the CRTC
  6164  5657 a00f                   ldy #15                                         ;
  6165                          write_CRTC_loop
  6166  5659 b9ba65                 lda register_CRTC_array,Y                       ; A = value to write
  6167  565c 8c00fe                 sty crtcAddressRegister                         ; Set CRTC address register to write into (0-15)
  6168  565f 8d01fe                 sta crtcAddressWrite                            ; Write new value into register
  6169  5662 88                     dey                                             ;
  6170  5663 10f4                   bpl write_CRTC_loop                             ;
  6171                          
  6172  5665 a252                   ldx #initial_zero_page_values_end - initial_zero_page_values - 1 ; Copy initial_zero_page_values to zero page
  6173                          copy_zero_page_values_loop                          ;
  6174  5667 bdca65                 lda initial_zero_page_values,X                  ;
  6175  566a 954d                   sta $4d,X                                       ;
  6176  566c ca                     dex                                             ;
  6177  566d 10f8                   bpl copy_zero_page_values_loop                  ;
  6178                          
  6179  566f a901                   lda #1                                          ;
  6180  5671 8517                   sta music_enabled                               ;
  6181  5673 a901                   lda #1                                          ;
  6182  5675 85d6                   sta tune_number                                 ;
  6183  5677 a900                   lda #0                                          ;
  6184  5679 a215                   ldx #sound_variables_end - sound_variables_start + 1 ;
  6185                          -
  6186  567b 9519                   sta sound_variables_start,X                     ;
  6187  567d ca                     dex                                             ;
  6188  567e 10fb                   bpl -                                           ;
  6189                          
  6190  5680 a97f                   LDA #$7f                                        ; }
  6191  5682 8d4efe                 STA systemVIAInterruptEnableRegister            ; } Disable all interrupts
  6192  5685 58                     cli                                             ;
  6193                          
  6194  5686 a984                   lda #<irq_routine                               ;
  6195  5688 8d0402                 sta irq1_vector_low                             ;
  6196  568b a953                   lda #>irq_routine                               ;
  6197  568d 8d0502                 sta irq1_vector_high                            ;
  6198                          
  6199  5690 a9c0                   lda #$c0                                        ; Enable timer 1
  6200  5692 8d4efe                 sta systemVIAInterruptEnableRegister            ; Interrupt enable register
  6201  5695 a9c0                   lda #$c0                                        ; Enable free run mode
  6202  5697 8d4bfe                 sta systemVIAAuxiliaryControlRegister           ; Auxiliary control register
  6203                          
  6204  569a a927                   lda #<Timer1Value                               ;
  6205  569c 8d44fe                 sta systemVIATimer1CounterLow                   ;
  6206                              ; Get high byte ready so we can write it as quickly as possible at the right moment
  6207  569f a213                   ldx #>Timer1Value                               ;
  6208                          
  6209                              ; Wait for VSync without having to catch it from its IRQ
  6210  56a1 a902                   lda #2                                          ;
  6211  56a3 8d4dfe                 sta systemVIAInterruptFlagRegister              ; clear VSync flag
  6212                          -
  6213  56a6 2c4dfe                 bit systemVIAInterruptFlagRegister              ;
  6214  56a9 f0fb                   beq -                                           ; poll VSync flag
  6215                          
  6216  56ab 8e45fe                 stx systemVIATimer1CounterHigh                  ; start Timer 1 counting
  6217  56ae 8d4dfe                 sta systemVIAInterruptFlagRegister              ; clear VSync flag
  6218                          
  6219                              ; Set timer to fire every 'short time' (set latch)
  6220  56b1 a9fe                   lda #<ShortTimerValue                           ;
  6221  56b3 8d46fe                 sta systemVIATimer1LatchLow                     ;
  6222  56b6 a901                   lda #>ShortTimerValue                           ;
  6223  56b8 8d47fe                 sta systemVIATimer1LatchHigh                    ;
  6224                          
  6225  56bb a900                   lda #0                                          ;
  6226  56bd 8500                   sta irq_counter                                 ;
  6227                          
  6228  56bf 4c8d4d                 jmp real_entry_point                            ;

  6528                          ; write first byte:   128 + 32*C + bottom four bits of pitch P (0-15)
  6529                          ; write second byte:  top 6 bits of pitch P
  6530                          !macro pitch_first_byte .pitch {
  6531                              !byte 128 + 32 * 0 + (.pitch % 16)
  6532                          }
  6533                          
  6534                          !macro pitch_second_byte .pitch {
  6535                              !byte .pitch / 16
  6536                          }
